Blog Platform → Cloudflare DNS Configuration #BP001\n* The domain \`52vibes.dev\` SHALL be configured with Cloudflare DNS.\n* A CNAME record SHALL point \`52vibes.dev\` to the Cloudflare Pages deployment URL (\`\u003cproject\u003e.pages.dev\`).\n* Cloudflare proxy (orange cloud) SHALL be enabled for CDN and SSL termination.\n* DNS propagation SHALL complete within 24 hours of configuration.\n* The \`www\` subdomain SHOULD redirect to the apex domain (\`52vibes.dev\`).\n* References:\n  + [Cloudflare Pages Custom Domains](https://developers.cloudflare.com/pages/configuration/custom-domains/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_DNS_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → DNS Resolution Verification #BP_DNS_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify DNS resolves correctly to Cloudflare Pages.\n* **Setup:** Configure DNS records in Cloudflare dashboard.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Run \`dig 52vibes.dev\` → Expect CNAME or A record pointing to Cloudflare\n  - TS2: Run \`dig www.52vibes.dev\` → Expect redirect record configured\n  - TS3: Query from multiple geographic locations → Expect consistent resolution\n  - TS4: Verify Cloudflare proxy status → Expect orange cloud enabled in dashboard\n* **Boundary Cases:**\n  - BC1: Test immediately after DNS change → Document propagation time\n  - BC2: Test from different ISPs → Expect consistent results after propagation\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_CFP_0001] - Blog Platform → Cloudflare Pages Project Configuration #BP001\n* A Cloudflare Pages project SHALL be created and linked to the GitHub repository.\n* Build configuration SHALL specify:\n  - Build command: \`hugo --minify\`\n  - Build output directory: \`public\`\n  - Root directory: \`/\` (repository root)\n  - Hugo version environment variable: \`HUGO_VERSION=0.139.0\`\n* Production branch SHALL be set to \`main\`.\n* Preview deployments SHALL be enabled for pull requests.\n* The project name SHALL result in a \`*.pages.dev\` URL that serves the site.\n* References:\n  + [Cloudflare Pages Hugo Framework Guide](https://developers.cloudflare.com/pages/framework-guides/deploy-a-hugo-site/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_CFP_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Cloudflare Pages Build Verification #BP_CFP_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify Cloudflare Pages builds and deploys successfully.\n* **Setup:** Link GitHub repository to Cloudflare Pages project.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Push commit to main branch → Expect build triggers automatically\n  - TS2: Monitor build logs → Expect Hugo build completes without errors\n  - TS3: Verify build output → Expect \`public/\` directory generated\n  - TS4: Access \`\u003cproject\u003e.pages.dev\` → Expect site accessible\n  - TS5: Verify HUGO_VERSION in build → Expect version 0.139.0 or higher\n* **Failure Cases:**\n  - FC1: Invalid Hugo config → Expect build fails with clear error\n  - FC2: Missing theme → Expect build fails, previous deployment remains live\n* **Performance:**\n  - Measure build duration → Expect under 2 minutes for initial build\n  - Measure deployment time → Expect under 1 minute after build\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_CFP_0002] - Blog Platform → Environment Variables #BP001\n* The following environment variables SHALL be configured in Cloudflare Pages:\n  - \`HUGO_VERSION\`: \`0.139.0\` (or latest stable)\n  - \`HUGO_ENVIRONMENT\`: \`production\` (for production builds)\n* Environment variables SHALL be set in Cloudflare Pages project settings.\n* No sensitive credentials SHALL be stored in environment variables for this project.\n* References:\n  + [Cloudflare Pages Environment Variables](https://developers.cloudflare.com/pages/configuration/build-configuration/#environment-variables)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_CFP_TEST_0002] - Blog Platform → Environment Variable Verification #BP_CFP_0002\n* **Objective:** Verify environment variables are correctly applied.\n* **Setup:** Configure environment variables in Cloudflare Pages dashboard.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Trigger build → Inspect build logs for HUGO_VERSION\n  - TS2: Verify Hugo version in output → Expect matches configured version\n  - TS3: Check production environment → Expect HUGO_ENVIRONMENT=production\n* **Verification:**\n  - Build log SHALL show \"Hugo v0.139.0\" or configured version\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_HUGO_0001] - Blog Platform → Hugo Base URL Configuration #BP001\n* Hugo configuration SHALL set \`baseURL\` to \`https://52vibes.dev/\`.\n* Hugo configuration file SHALL be \`hugo.toml\` (TOML format preferred).\n* The blog section SHALL be configured to serve content from \`/blog/\` path.\n* Configuration SHALL include:\n  - \`languageCode\`: \`en-us\`\n  - \`title\`: \`52 Vibes\`\n  - \`enableRobotsTXT\`: \`true\`\n  - \`enableGitInfo\`: \`true\` (for lastmod dates)\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Configuration](https://gohugo.io/getting-started/configuration/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_HUGO_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Base URL and Path Verification #BP_HUGO_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify Hugo generates correct URLs and paths.\n* **Setup:** Build site locally with \`hugo --minify\`.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Inspect generated HTML → Expect all URLs use \`https://52vibes.dev/\`\n  - TS2: Verify blog index path → Expect accessible at \`/blog/\`\n  - TS3: Check canonical URLs → Expect \`\u003clink rel=\"canonical\"\u003e\` uses correct base\n  - TS4: Verify internal links → Expect no broken internal links\n  - TS5: Check sitemap.xml → Expect all URLs use production base URL\n* **Local vs Production:**\n  - Local development MAY use \`localhost:1313\`\n  - Production build MUST use \`https://52vibes.dev/\`\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_SSL_0001] - Blog Platform → HTTPS and SSL Configuration #BP001\n* All traffic SHALL be served over HTTPS.\n* HTTP requests SHALL redirect to HTTPS (301 permanent redirect).\n* SSL certificate SHALL be automatically provisioned by Cloudflare.\n* SSL mode SHALL be set to \"Full (strict)\" in Cloudflare settings.\n* HSTS (HTTP Strict Transport Security) SHOULD be enabled.\n* References:\n  + [Cloudflare SSL/TLS](https://developers.cloudflare.com/ssl/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_SSL_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → HTTPS and Certificate Verification #BP_SSL_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify SSL/TLS is correctly configured.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Request \`http://52vibes.dev/blog\` → Expect 301 redirect to HTTPS\n  - TS2: Request \`https://52vibes.dev/blog\` → Expect HTTP 200\n  - TS3: Inspect certificate → Expect valid, issued by Cloudflare\n  - TS4: Check certificate expiry → Expect auto-renewal configured\n  - TS5: Test with SSL Labs → Expect A or A+ rating\n* **Security Headers:**\n  - Verify HSTS header present (if enabled)\n  - Check for secure cookies (if any)\n* **References:**\n  + [SSL Labs Server Test](https://www.ssllabs.com/ssltest/)\n\n### Core Architecture (BP002, BP003, BP004)\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_SSR_0001] - Blog Platform → Server-Side Rendering Architecture #BP002\n* All page content SHALL be rendered at build time by Hugo (Static Site Generation).\n* HTML output SHALL contain complete content without requiring JavaScript hydration.\n* No client-side templating frameworks (React, Vue, etc.) SHALL be used.\n* Hugo templates SHALL use Go template syntax for content rendering.\n* Template directory structure SHALL follow Hugo conventions:\n  - \`layouts/_default/baseof.html\` - base template\n  - \`layouts/_default/single.html\` - single content pages\n  - \`layouts/_default/list.html\` - list/index pages\n  - \`layouts/partials/\` - reusable template components\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Templates](https://gohugo.io/templates/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_SSR_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Static Rendering Verification #BP_SSR_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify all content is statically rendered.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Build site with \`hugo --minify\` → Inspect \`public/\` directory\n  - TS2: Open any HTML file → Expect complete content in source\n  - TS3: Disable JavaScript in browser → Load page → Expect all content visible\n  - TS4: Use \`curl\` to fetch page → Expect complete HTML in response\n  - TS5: Check for hydration scripts → Expect none present\n* **Content Types:**\n  - Test blog post pages\n  - Test index/list pages\n  - Test static pages (About, etc.)\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_NOJS_0001] - Blog Platform → JavaScript Budget and Constraints #BP002\n* Total JavaScript payload SHALL NOT exceed 2KB (minified, uncompressed).\n* JavaScript SHALL be used ONLY for:\n  - Theme toggle persistence (localStorage) - ~500 bytes\n  - Community page GitHub API fetch - ~1KB\n* No JavaScript frameworks or libraries SHALL be included.\n* All JavaScript SHALL be inline (no external JS files) or in a single bundled file.\n* JavaScript SHALL use vanilla ES6+ syntax (no transpilation required for modern browsers).\n* References:\n  + [JavaScript Module Best Practices](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Guide/Modules)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_NOJS_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → JavaScript Budget Verification #BP_NOJS_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify JavaScript stays within budget.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Build production site → Locate all JavaScript in output\n  - TS2: Measure total JS size → Expect ≤2KB minified\n  - TS3: List all JS functionality → Expect only theme toggle + API fetch\n  - TS4: Check for framework code → Expect none (React, Vue, jQuery, etc.)\n  - TS5: Verify ES6+ syntax → Expect no transpilation artifacts\n* **Tools:**\n  - Use browser DevTools Network tab\n  - Use \`wc -c\` on minified JS files\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_GRACE_0001] - Blog Platform → Graceful Degradation Strategy #BP002\n* When JavaScript is disabled:\n  - Theme SHALL default to system preference via \`prefers-color-scheme\`\n  - Theme toggle control SHALL remain visible but non-functional\n  - Community page SHALL display fallback link to GitHub topics page\n* No \"JavaScript required\" messages SHALL be displayed.\n* No broken layouts or missing content SHALL occur without JavaScript.\n* All navigation SHALL remain fully functional without JavaScript.\n* References:\n  + [Progressive Enhancement](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Glossary/Progressive_Enhancement)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_GRACE_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Graceful Degradation Verification #BP_GRACE_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify site functions correctly without JavaScript.\n* **Setup:** Disable JavaScript in browser settings.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Load blog index → Expect all posts listed, readable\n  - TS2: Navigate between pages → Expect all links work\n  - TS3: Check theme → Expect matches system preference\n  - TS4: View theme toggle → Expect visible (may be non-functional)\n  - TS5: Load Community page → Expect fallback content/link displayed\n  - TS6: Check for error messages → Expect none\n* **Browsers:**\n  - Test in Chrome, Firefox with JS disabled\n  - Test in lynx (inherently no JS)\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_RESP_0001] - Blog Platform → Responsive Breakpoint System #BP003\n* CSS SHALL implement the following breakpoint system:\n  - Mobile: \`max-width: 767px\`\n  - Tablet: \`min-width: 768px\` and \`max-width: 1023px\`\n  - Desktop: \`min-width: 1024px\`\n  - Large Desktop: \`min-width: 1440px\` (optional enhancement)\n* Breakpoints SHALL be defined as CSS custom properties or SCSS variables.\n* Mobile-first approach SHALL be used (base styles for mobile, media queries for larger).\n* No horizontal scrolling SHALL occur at any viewport width ≥320px.\n* References:\n  + [CSS Media Queries](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/CSS_media_queries)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_RESP_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Breakpoint Behavior Verification #BP_RESP_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify responsive behavior at all breakpoints.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Set viewport to 320px width → Expect no horizontal scroll, content readable\n  - TS2: Set viewport to 375px width → Expect mobile layout\n  - TS3: Set viewport to 768px width → Expect tablet layout transition\n  - TS4: Set viewport to 1024px width → Expect desktop layout\n  - TS5: Set viewport to 1920px width → Expect full desktop layout\n  - TS6: Resize viewport dynamically → Expect smooth transitions\n* **Orientation:**\n  - Test mobile viewports in portrait and landscape\n* **Content Types:**\n  - Test with long code blocks\n  - Test with tables\n  - Test with images\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_RESP_0002] - Blog Platform → Fluid Typography and Spacing #BP003\n* Typography SHALL scale fluidly using CSS \`clamp()\` function.\n* Base font size range: \`clamp(16px, 2.5vw, 18px)\` for body text.\n* Heading sizes SHALL scale proportionally.\n* Spacing (margins, padding) SHALL use relative units (rem, em) or viewport units.\n* Line length SHALL be constrained to 65-75 characters for readability.\n* References:\n  + [CSS clamp()](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/clamp)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_RESP_TEST_0002] - Blog Platform → Typography Scaling Verification #BP_RESP_0002\n* **Objective:** Verify typography scales appropriately.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Inspect body font size at 320px viewport → Expect ~16px\n  - TS2: Inspect body font size at 1920px viewport → Expect ~18px\n  - TS3: Measure line length in characters → Expect 65-75 characters max\n  - TS4: Check heading hierarchy → Expect proportional scaling\n  - TS5: Verify relative units in CSS → Expect rem/em usage\n* **Readability:**\n  - Verify text is readable at all viewport sizes\n  - Verify adequate spacing between elements\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_PERF_0001] - Blog Platform → Asset Optimization Pipeline #BP004\n* Hugo asset pipeline SHALL be configured for optimization:\n  - CSS: Minification enabled, unused CSS removal (if using SCSS)\n  - HTML: Minification via \`hugo --minify\`\n  - Images: WebP conversion with fallback, responsive srcset generation\n* Total page weight targets:\n  - Blog index: ≤500KB\n  - Blog post (without images): ≤300KB\n  - Any page with images: ≤800KB\n* Asset fingerprinting SHALL be enabled for cache busting.\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Asset Minification](https://gohugo.io/hugo-pipes/minification/)\n  + [Hugo Image Processing](https://gohugo.io/content-management/image-processing/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_PERF_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Asset Optimization Verification #BP_PERF_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify assets are properly optimized.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Build with \`hugo --minify\` → Verify minification applied\n  - TS2: Inspect CSS output → Expect minified (no whitespace/comments)\n  - TS3: Inspect HTML output → Expect minified\n  - TS4: Check image formats → Expect WebP with fallbacks\n  - TS5: Measure page weights → Verify within budget\n  - TS6: Check asset URLs → Expect fingerprinted filenames\n* **Tools:**\n  - Use browser DevTools Network tab for size measurements\n  - Use \`du -h\` on output files\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_PERF_0002] - Blog Platform → Core Web Vitals Optimization #BP004\n* Largest Contentful Paint (LCP) SHALL be under 2.5 seconds.\n* First Input Delay (FID) SHALL be under 100ms.\n* Cumulative Layout Shift (CLS) SHALL be under 0.1.\n* First Contentful Paint (FCP) SHOULD be under 1.5 seconds.\n* Implementation strategies:\n  - Preload critical fonts\n  - Inline critical CSS\n  - Defer non-critical resources\n  - Reserve space for dynamic content (prevent layout shifts)\n* References:\n  + [Core Web Vitals](https://web.dev/vitals/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_PERF_TEST_0002] - Blog Platform → Core Web Vitals Measurement #BP_PERF_0002\n* **Objective:** Verify Core Web Vitals meet targets.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Run Lighthouse on blog index → Expect Performance ≥95\n  - TS2: Measure LCP → Expect \u003c2.5s\n  - TS3: Measure FID → Expect \u003c100ms\n  - TS4: Measure CLS → Expect \u003c0.1\n  - TS5: Measure FCP → Expect \u003c1.5s\n  - TS6: Run on multiple page types → Expect consistent scores\n* **Testing Conditions:**\n  - Test with throttled connection (Slow 4G)\n  - Test with CPU throttling (4x slowdown)\n* **Tools:**\n  - Chrome DevTools Lighthouse\n  - WebPageTest.org\n  - PageSpeed Insights\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_PERF_0003] - Blog Platform → Font Loading Strategy #BP004\n* Fonts SHALL be loaded from Google Fonts CDN.\n* Font loading SHALL use \`font-display: swap\` to prevent invisible text.\n* Font preconnect hints SHALL be included in \`\u003chead\u003e\`:\n  - \`\u003clink rel=\"preconnect\" href=\"https://fonts.googleapis.com\"\u003e\`\n  - \`\u003clink rel=\"preconnect\" href=\"https://fonts.gstatic.com\" crossorigin\u003e\`\n* Font families to load:\n  - IBM Plex Sans: weights 400, 500, 600, 700\n  - JetBrains Mono: weight 400\n* Font subsetting SHOULD be applied (latin subset only for initial load).\n* References:\n  + [Google Fonts CSS API](https://developers.google.com/fonts/docs/css2)\n  + [font-display](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/@font-face/font-display)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_PERF_TEST_0003] - Blog Platform → Font Loading Verification #BP_PERF_0003\n* **Objective:** Verify fonts load efficiently without blocking render.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Inspect \`\u003chead\u003e\` → Expect preconnect hints for Google Fonts\n  - TS2: Check font-display → Expect \`swap\` in font declarations\n  - TS3: Block Google Fonts → Expect fallback fonts display immediately\n  - TS4: Measure font load time → Expect \u003c500ms on fast connection\n  - TS5: Check for FOIT (Flash of Invisible Text) → Expect none\n  - TS6: Check for FOUT (Flash of Unstyled Text) → Acceptable with swap\n* **Network Tab:**\n  - Verify font files loaded from fonts.gstatic.com\n  - Verify only required weights loaded\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_DEPLOY_0001] - Blog Platform → Deployment Time Constraints #BP005\n* Content-only changes SHALL deploy within 5 minutes of push to main branch.\n* Full site rebuilds SHALL complete within 10 minutes.\n* Cloudflare Pages build SHALL NOT require manual intervention.\n* Build failures SHALL NOT affect live production site (atomic deployments).\n* Deployment notifications SHOULD be available via Cloudflare dashboard.\n* References:\n  + [Cloudflare Pages Deployments](https://developers.cloudflare.com/pages/get-started/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_DEPLOY_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Deployment Time Verification #BP_DEPLOY_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify deployment completes within time constraints.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Push content-only change (markdown file) → Start timer\n  - TS2: Monitor Cloudflare Pages deployment → Record completion time\n  - TS3: Verify deployed content → Expect change visible\n  - TS4: Calculate total time → Expect ≤5 minutes\n* **Failure Recovery:**\n  - Push invalid change → Verify build fails\n  - Verify live site unchanged → Previous version still served\n* **Metrics:**\n  - Document average build times over 10 deployments\n\n### CLI Browser Compatibility (BP006)\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_CLI_0001] - Blog Platform → Semantic HTML for CLI Rendering #BP006\n* HTML structure SHALL prioritize semantic elements that render well in text browsers.\n* Required semantic elements:\n  - \`\u003cheader\u003e\` for site header\n  - \`\u003cnav\u003e\` for navigation with \`\u003cul\u003e\` list structure\n  - \`\u003cmain\u003e\` for primary content\n  - \`\u003carticle\u003e\` for blog posts\n  - \`\u003csection\u003e\` for content sections with headings\n  - \`\u003cfooter\u003e\` for site footer\n* Links SHALL use descriptive text (no \"click here\").\n* Images SHALL include meaningful \`alt\` text for text-only display.\n* References:\n  + [HTML Semantic Elements](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Glossary/Semantics#semantics_in_html)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_CLI_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Lynx Rendering Verification #BP_CLI_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify site renders correctly in lynx browser.\n* **Setup:** Install lynx text browser.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: \`lynx https://52vibes.dev/blog\` → Expect page loads, title visible\n  - TS2: Navigate to blog post → Expect content fully readable\n  - TS3: Follow navigation links → Expect all work correctly\n  - TS4: Check TOC anchor links → Expect navigate to sections\n  - TS5: View post with code blocks → Expect code readable\n  - TS6: Check for broken elements → Expect none\n* **Content Verification:**\n  - Verify all text content visible\n  - Verify links clearly labeled\n  - Verify image alt text displayed\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_CLI_TEST_0002] - Blog Platform → w3m Rendering Verification #BP_CLI_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify site renders correctly in w3m browser.\n* **Setup:** Install w3m text browser.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: \`w3m https://52vibes.dev/blog\` → Expect page loads\n  - TS2: Navigate to Weekly Index → Expect table renders readably\n  - TS3: Verify table alignment → Expect columns aligned\n  - TS4: Follow navigation links → Expect all work correctly\n  - TS5: Test forms (if any) → Expect usable\n* **Table Testing:**\n  - Weekly Index table with 52 weeks → Must be readable\n  - Tables in blog posts → Must render with structure\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_CLI_0002] - Blog Platform → Table Rendering Strategy #BP006\n* Tables SHALL use standard HTML \`\u003ctable\u003e\` elements with proper structure.\n* Required table elements:\n  - \`\u003cthead\u003e\` with \`\u003cth\u003e\` headers for accessibility\n  - \`\u003ctbody\u003e\` for data rows\n  - \`scope\` attributes on header cells\n* Tables SHALL NOT use CSS grid/flexbox to simulate tables.\n* Complex tables SHOULD include \`\u003ccaption\u003e\` for context.\n* Very wide tables MAY use horizontal scroll container on mobile (CSS only).\n* For CLI browsers, tables SHALL degrade to readable text columns.\n* References:\n  + [HTML Table Accessibility](https://www.w3.org/WAI/tutorials/tables/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_CLI_TEST_0003] - Blog Platform → Table Accessibility Verification #BP_CLI_0002\n* **Objective:** Verify tables are accessible and CLI-friendly.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Inspect Weekly Index table HTML → Expect \`\u003cthead\u003e\`, \`\u003ctbody\u003e\`, \`\u003cth\u003e\`\n  - TS2: Check \`scope\` attributes → Expect on header cells\n  - TS3: Test in screen reader → Expect headers announced\n  - TS4: Test in w3m → Expect table structure preserved\n  - TS5: Test in lynx → Expect readable (may linearize)\n* **Mobile:**\n  - Test table at 320px viewport → Verify readable without breaking layout\n\n### Visual Design System (BP007, BP008, BP009, BP010, BP011)\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_TMUX_0001] - Blog Platform → Tmux-Inspired Layout Structure #BP007\n* Page layout SHALL implement a tmux-inspired terminal aesthetic:\n  - Top status bar: Fixed height, full width, contains week numbers\n  - Main content pane: Bordered frame containing page content\n  - Bottom navigation bar: Fixed height, full width, contains nav links\n* CSS borders SHALL create the framed appearance (no ASCII characters).\n* Border style SHALL be \`solid 1px\` using theme colors.\n* Content pane SHOULD have subtle inner padding (1-2rem).\n* Layout SHALL remain consistent across all page types.\n* References:\n  + [tmux Manual](https://man7.org/linux/man-pages/man1/tmux.1.html) (for aesthetic reference)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_TMUX_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Tmux Layout Verification #BP_TMUX_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify tmux-inspired visual design.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Load any page → Verify top status bar present\n  - TS2: Verify main content area → Expect bordered frame\n  - TS3: Verify bottom navigation → Expect navigation bar present\n  - TS4: Compare to tmux screenshot → Expect similar aesthetic\n  - TS5: Test multiple pages → Expect consistent layout\n* **Visual Elements:**\n  - Status bar contains week numbers (clickable for completed weeks)\n  - Main pane has visible border\n  - Navigation bar at bottom with links\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_GRUVBOX_0001] - Blog Platform → Gruvbox Color Palette Implementation #BP008\n* Color system SHALL be based on Gruvbox color palette.\n* CSS custom properties SHALL define all colors:\n  \`\`\`css\n  /* Dark theme */\n  --bg-dark: #1d2021;\n  --bg-dark-soft: #282828;\n  --fg-dark: #ebdbb2;\n  --accent: #d65d0e;\n  --green: #b8bb26;\n  --red: #fb4934;\n  --yellow: #fabd2f;\n  --blue: #83a598;\n  \n  /* Light theme */\n  --bg-light: #fbf1c7;\n  --bg-light-soft: #f2e5bc;\n  --fg-light: #3c3836;\n  \`\`\`\n* All UI elements SHALL use these CSS custom properties (no hardcoded colors).\n* Accent color (#d65d0e orange) SHALL be used for interactive elements.\n* References:\n  + [Gruvbox GitHub](https://github.com/morhetz/gruvbox)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_GRUVBOX_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Color Palette Verification #BP_GRUVBOX_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify Gruvbox colors are correctly implemented.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Inspect CSS → Expect custom properties defined\n  - TS2: Dark mode background → Sample color → Expect #1d2021 or similar\n  - TS3: Light mode background → Sample color → Expect #fbf1c7 or similar\n  - TS4: Dark mode text → Sample color → Expect #ebdbb2 or similar\n  - TS5: Light mode text → Sample color → Expect #3c3836 or similar\n  - TS6: Accent color (links, buttons) → Expect #d65d0e\n* **Tools:**\n  - Use browser color picker DevTools\n  - Verify CSS custom properties in computed styles\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_THEME_0001] - Blog Platform → CSS Theme Switching Mechanism #BP008\n* Default theme SHALL be determined by \`prefers-color-scheme\` media query.\n* CSS SHALL use media query to apply theme-specific custom properties:\n  \`\`\`css\n  :root {\n    /* Light theme defaults */\n  }\n  @media (prefers-color-scheme: dark) {\n    :root {\n      /* Dark theme overrides */\n    }\n  }\n  \`\`\`\n* A \`data-theme\` attribute on \`\u003chtml\u003e\` element SHALL allow JavaScript override.\n* When \`data-theme=\"dark\"\` or \`data-theme=\"light\"\` is set, it SHALL override system preference.\n* Theme transition SHALL NOT cause layout shift (CLS).\n* References:\n  + [prefers-color-scheme](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/@media/prefers-color-scheme)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_THEME_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Theme Switching Verification #BP_THEME_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify CSS theme switching works correctly.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Set OS to dark mode → Load page → Expect dark theme\n  - TS2: Set OS to light mode → Load page → Expect light theme\n  - TS3: Set \`data-theme=\"dark\"\` in DevTools → Expect dark theme override\n  - TS4: Set \`data-theme=\"light\"\` in DevTools → Expect light theme override\n  - TS5: Toggle system preference → Expect theme updates (if no JS override)\n* **No JavaScript:**\n  - Disable JS → Verify theme follows system preference\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_TOGGLE_0001] - Blog Platform → Theme Toggle Implementation #BP009\n* A visible toggle control SHALL be placed in the page header or footer.\n* Toggle SHALL be implemented as a \`\u003cbutton\u003e\` element for accessibility.\n* Toggle SHALL have appropriate ARIA attributes:\n  - \`aria-label\`: \"Toggle dark/light theme\"\n  - \`aria-pressed\`: \"true\" or \"false\" based on state\n* Clicking toggle SHALL:\n  1. Set \`data-theme\` attribute on \`\u003chtml\u003e\`\n  2. Store preference in localStorage key \`theme\`\n  3. Update button visual state\n* JavaScript for toggle SHALL be under 500 bytes minified.\n* References:\n  + [ARIA button pattern](https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/button/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_TOGGLE_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Theme Toggle Functionality #BP_TOGGLE_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify theme toggle works and persists preference.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Locate toggle button → Expect visible in header/footer\n  - TS2: Click toggle in dark mode → Expect switch to light\n  - TS3: Click toggle in light mode → Expect switch to dark\n  - TS4: Inspect localStorage → Expect \`theme\` key set\n  - TS5: Refresh page → Expect preference persisted\n  - TS6: Close browser, reopen → Expect preference persisted\n* **Accessibility:**\n  - TS7: Inspect \`aria-label\` → Expect descriptive label\n  - TS8: Tab to toggle → Expect focusable\n  - TS9: Press Enter on focused toggle → Expect theme change\n  - TS10: Check \`aria-pressed\` → Expect updates with state\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_TOGGLE_0002] - Blog Platform → Theme Preference Persistence #BP009\n* Theme preference SHALL be stored in localStorage under key \`theme\`.\n* Valid values: \`\"dark\"\`, \`\"light\"\`, or absent (system preference).\n* On page load, JavaScript SHALL:\n  1. Check localStorage for \`theme\` value\n  2. If set, apply \`data-theme\` attribute\n  3. If not set, defer to CSS \`prefers-color-scheme\`\n* Theme restoration SHALL occur before first paint (inline script in \`\u003chead\u003e\`).\n* This prevents flash of wrong theme on page load.\n* References:\n  + [localStorage API](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Window/localStorage)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_TOGGLE_TEST_0002] - Blog Platform → Theme Persistence Edge Cases #BP_TOGGLE_0002\n* **Objective:** Verify theme persistence handles edge cases.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Clear localStorage → Load page → Expect system preference\n  - TS2: Set theme → Load new page → Expect theme persists\n  - TS3: Set theme → Hard refresh (Ctrl+Shift+R) → Expect theme persists\n  - TS4: Set invalid localStorage value → Load page → Expect graceful fallback\n  - TS5: localStorage unavailable → Load page → Expect system preference\n* **Flash Prevention:**\n  - TS6: Set dark preference → Load page → Expect NO flash of light theme\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_TYPO_0001] - Blog Platform → Typography System Implementation #BP010\n* Font family stack SHALL be defined in CSS custom properties:\n  \`\`\`css\n  --font-body: 'IBM Plex Sans', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif;\n  --font-mono: 'JetBrains Mono', 'SF Mono', 'Menlo', monospace;\n  \`\`\`\n* Font sizes SHALL use a modular scale (ratio ~1.25):\n  - \`--font-size-sm\`: 0.875rem (14px)\n  - \`--font-size-base\`: 1rem (16px)\n  - \`--font-size-lg\`: 1.125rem (18px)\n  - \`--font-size-xl\`: 1.25rem (20px)\n  - \`--font-size-2xl\`: 1.5rem (24px)\n  - \`--font-size-3xl\`: 2rem (32px)\n* Line height for body text SHALL be 1.6-1.7 for readability.\n* References:\n  + [Modular Scale](https://www.modularscale.com/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_TYPO_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Typography Implementation Verification #BP_TYPO_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify correct fonts and sizes are applied.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Inspect body text → Expect IBM Plex Sans\n  - TS2: Inspect headings → Expect IBM Plex Sans\n  - TS3: Inspect code blocks → Expect JetBrains Mono\n  - TS4: Inspect inline code → Expect JetBrains Mono\n  - TS5: Check body font size → Expect 16-18px\n  - TS6: Check line height → Expect 1.6-1.7\n* **Fallback:**\n  - Block Google Fonts → Expect system fonts render cleanly\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_BORDER_0001] - Blog Platform → CSS Border System #BP011\n* All visual borders SHALL be implemented using CSS \`border\` properties.\n* ASCII box-drawing characters SHALL NOT be used for structural elements.\n* Border colors SHALL use CSS custom properties for theme compatibility.\n* Standard border definition:\n  \`\`\`css\n  --border-color: var(--fg-dark); /* or --fg-light */\n  --border-width: 1px;\n  --border-style: solid;\n  \`\`\`\n* Border radius SHALL be minimal or zero for terminal aesthetic.\n* References:\n  + [CSS Borders](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/border)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_BORDER_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Border Implementation Verification #BP_BORDER_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify CSS borders, not ASCII characters.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Inspect page HTML source → Search for box-drawing Unicode (─│┌┐└┘)\n  - TS2: Expect NOT found in structural elements\n  - TS3: Inspect border elements via DevTools → Expect CSS border properties\n  - TS4: Toggle theme → Expect borders visible in both themes\n  - TS5: Test in CLI browser → Expect readable without borders\n* **Unicode Check:**\n  - Search: U+2500-U+257F (Box Drawing block)\n  - These MAY appear in content, but NOT for layout\n\n### Navigation System (BP012, BP013, BP014, BP015, BP016)\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_NAV_0001] - Blog Platform → Week Status Bar Implementation #BP012\n* Top status bar SHALL display week numbers 1-52.\n* Week numbers SHALL be generated by Hugo template from content data.\n* Implementation SHALL use Hugo's \`.Site.Pages\` to determine completed weeks.\n* Completed weeks SHALL render as \`\u003ca\u003e\` links to post URLs.\n* Incomplete weeks SHALL render as \`\u003cspan\u003e\` elements (not clickable).\n* Visual styling SHALL distinguish clickable vs non-clickable weeks.\n* Week numbers SHALL be displayed in a single horizontal row (with wrapping on mobile).\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Page Collections](https://gohugo.io/templates/lists/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_NAV_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Week Status Bar Verification #BP_NAV_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify week status bar displays correctly.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Load any page → Verify status bar at top\n  - TS2: Count week numbers → Expect 52 visible\n  - TS3: Identify completed weeks → Verify are \`\u003ca\u003e\` links\n  - TS4: Identify incomplete weeks → Verify are NOT links\n  - TS5: Click completed week → Expect navigates to post\n  - TS6: Attempt click incomplete week → Expect no navigation\n* **Visual:**\n  - Completed weeks: colored/underlined\n  - Incomplete weeks: muted/no interaction indicator\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_NAV_0002] - Blog Platform → Week Tooltip Implementation #BP013\n* Week number links SHALL include \`title\` attribute with post title.\n* Tooltip SHALL use native browser tooltip (no JavaScript).\n* Hugo template SHALL populate title from front matter.\n* Example: \`\u003ca href=\"/blog/week-01-infrastructure/\" title=\"Week 1: Infrastructure\"\u003e1\u003c/a\u003e\`\n* Incomplete weeks SHALL NOT have tooltips.\n* References:\n  + [HTML title attribute](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Global_attributes/title)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_NAV_TEST_0002] - Blog Platform → Week Tooltip Verification #BP_NAV_0002\n* **Objective:** Verify native tooltips on week links.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Hover over completed week number → Expect tooltip appears\n  - TS2: Verify tooltip content → Expect post title displayed\n  - TS3: Hover over incomplete week → Expect NO tooltip\n  - TS4: Inspect HTML → Expect \`title\` attribute on completed week links\n  - TS5: Verify no JavaScript tooltip → Expect native browser behavior\n* **Timing:**\n  - Tooltip appears after browser default delay (~500-1000ms)\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_NAV_0003] - Blog Platform → Weeks Index Link #BP014\n* Status bar SHALL include \"Weeks\" label/link.\n* Link SHALL navigate to \`/blog/weeks/\` (Weekly Index page).\n* Implementation SHALL be standard \`\u003ca\u003e\` element.\n* Link SHALL be accessible in CLI browsers.\n* Position SHALL be consistent (e.g., left side of status bar).\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Internal Links](https://gohugo.io/content-management/cross-references/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_NAV_TEST_0003] - Blog Platform → Weeks Index Link Verification #BP_NAV_0003\n* **Objective:** Verify \"Weeks\" link in status bar.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Locate \"Weeks\" in status bar → Expect visible\n  - TS2: Click \"Weeks\" → Expect navigates to \`/blog/weeks/\`\n  - TS3: Inspect HTML → Expect \`\u003ca\u003e\` element\n  - TS4: Test in lynx → Expect link accessible and functional\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_NAV_0004] - Blog Platform → Footer Navigation Bar #BP015\n* Footer navigation bar SHALL be present on all pages.\n* Required links:\n  - About: \`/about/\`\n  - Weekly Index: \`/blog/weeks/\`\n  - Reports: \`/blog/reports/\`\n  - RSS: \`/index.xml\` or \`/blog/index.xml\`\n  - GitHub: \`https://github.com/\u003cowner\u003e/\u003crepo\u003e\` (external)\n* Links SHALL be implemented as \`\u003ca\u003e\` elements within \`\u003cnav\u003e\` and \`\u003cfooter\u003e\`.\n* Link order SHALL be consistent across all pages.\n* Hugo partial template SHALL render footer navigation.\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Partials](https://gohugo.io/templates/partials/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_NAV_TEST_0004] - Blog Platform → Footer Navigation Verification #BP_NAV_0004\n* **Objective:** Verify footer navigation completeness.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Load blog index → Verify footer nav present\n  - TS2: Verify About link → Expect navigates to \`/about/\`\n  - TS3: Verify Weekly Index link → Expect navigates to \`/blog/weeks/\`\n  - TS4: Verify Reports link → Expect navigates to \`/blog/reports/\`\n  - TS5: Verify RSS link → Expect valid RSS feed\n  - TS6: Verify GitHub link → Expect opens GitHub repository\n  - TS7: Test on About page → Expect same footer nav\n  - TS8: Test on blog post → Expect same footer nav\n* **External Links:**\n  - GitHub link SHOULD open in new tab (optional \`target=\"_blank\"\`)\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_NAV_0005] - Blog Platform → Descriptive Navigation Labels #BP016\n* All navigation links SHALL use descriptive text labels.\n* Icons MAY accompany labels but SHALL NOT replace them.\n* Prohibited patterns:\n  - \"Click here\"\n  - \"Read more\"\n  - Icon-only links\n  - Single character links (except week numbers in status bar)\n* Week numbers in status bar SHALL have title attribute for context.\n* External links SHOULD indicate they open externally.\n* References:\n  + [WCAG Link Purpose](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG21/Understanding/link-purpose-in-context.html)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_NAV_TEST_0005] - TS2: Search for \"click here\" → Expect NOT found\n  - TS3: Search for \"read more\" → Expect NOT found\n  - TS4: Check icon-only elements → Expect none in navigation\n  - TS5: Test in lynx → Expect navigation understandable\n  - TS6: Run accessibility audit → Expect no \"link purpose\" violations\n\n### Table of Contents (BP017, BP018)\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_TOC_0001] - Blog Platform → Auto-Generated TOC Implementation #BP017\n* Table of Contents SHALL be auto-generated from post headings.\n* Hugo's \`.TableOfContents\` function SHALL be used.\n* TOC SHALL include h2 and h3 headings.\n* Configuration in \`hugo.toml\`:\n  \`\`\`toml\n  [markup.tableOfContents]\n    startLevel = 2\n    endLevel = 3\n    ordered = false\n  \`\`\`\n* TOC SHALL be rendered as nested \`\u003cul\u003e\` lists.\n* Each TOC item SHALL link to corresponding heading anchor.\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Table of Contents](https://gohugo.io/content-management/toc/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_TOC_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → TOC Generation Verification #BP_TOC_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify TOC is correctly generated.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Create post with h2 and h3 headings → Build site\n  - TS2: Verify TOC appears at top of post → Expect \`\u003cul\u003e\` structure\n  - TS3: Count TOC items → Expect matches heading count\n  - TS4: Click TOC item → Expect scrolls to section\n  - TS5: Verify URL hash → Expect \`#heading-id\` in URL\n  - TS6: Test with nested headings (h3 under h2) → Expect nested list\n* **Edge Cases:**\n  - Post with no headings → TOC section empty or hidden\n  - Post with only h1 headings → TOC should be empty\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_TOC_0002] - Blog Platform → Heading Anchor IDs #BP017\n* All h2 and h3 headings SHALL have auto-generated IDs.\n* Hugo SHALL generate IDs using the \`anchorize\` function.\n* IDs SHALL be URL-safe (lowercase, hyphenated).\n* Duplicate heading text SHALL result in unique IDs (suffix numbers).\n* Example: \"Getting Started\" → id=\"getting-started\"\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Heading Anchors](https://gohugo.io/getting-started/configuration-markup/#heading)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_TOC_TEST_0002] - Blog Platform → Heading Anchor Verification #BP_TOC_0002\n* **Objective:** Verify heading anchors are correctly generated.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Inspect h2 element → Expect \`id\` attribute present\n  - TS2: Verify ID format → Expect lowercase, hyphenated\n  - TS3: Test duplicate headings → Expect unique IDs (suffix)\n  - TS4: Navigate to \`#heading-id\` URL → Expect scrolls to heading\n  - TS5: Test with special characters → Expect sanitized ID\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_STICKY_0001] - Blog Platform → CSS Sticky Section Indicator #BP018\n* Section indicator SHOULD be implemented using CSS \`position: sticky\`.\n* Indicator SHALL display current section name during scroll.\n* Implementation SHALL NOT require JavaScript.\n* CSS scroll-snap or IntersectionObserver-free approach SHALL be used.\n* This is a SHOULD requirement; implementation is optional.\n* If implemented, format: \"§ Reading: [Section Name]\"\n* References:\n  + [CSS position: sticky](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/position)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_STICKY_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Sticky Section Indicator Verification #BP_STICKY_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify sticky section indicator (if implemented).\n* **Test Steps (if implemented):**\n  - TS1: Navigate to long post (5+ sections) → Locate indicator\n  - TS2: Scroll through sections → Expect indicator updates\n  - TS3: Verify CSS position → Expect \`sticky\`\n  - TS4: Disable JavaScript → Expect indicator still works\n  - TS5: Verify format → Expect \"§ Reading: [Section Name]\"\n* **Note:** SHOULD requirement; document if not implemented\n\n### Content Pages (BP019, BP020, BP021, BP022, BP023)\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_ABOUT_0001] - Blog Platform → About Page Implementation #BP019\n* About page SHALL be created at \`content/about/_index.md\`.\n* Page SHALL use Hugo \`page\` layout.\n* Required content sections:\n  - Project description (52vibes purpose)\n  - Author information\n  - Contact/contribution information\n* URL SHALL be \`/about/\`.\n* Page SHALL use same layout/styling as blog pages.\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Content Organization](https://gohugo.io/content-management/organization/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_ABOUT_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → About Page Verification #BP_ABOUT_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify About page content and accessibility.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Navigate to \`/about/\` → Expect HTTP 200\n  - TS2: Verify project description → Expect meaningful content\n  - TS3: Verify author information → Expect name/details\n  - TS4: Verify layout matches blog → Expect consistent design\n  - TS5: Test in CLI browser → Expect content readable\n* **Content Quality:**\n  - Description explains 52vibes project\n  - Author section has appropriate detail\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_WEEKLY_0001] - Blog Platform → Weekly Index Page Implementation #BP020\n* Weekly Index page SHALL be created at \`content/blog/weeks/_index.md\`.\n* Page SHALL display table of all 52 weeks.\n* Table columns: Week #, Status, Title, Date Published.\n* Hugo template SHALL iterate \`.Site.Pages\` to build table.\n* Status values: Completed (linked), In Progress (labeled), Upcoming (muted).\n* Table SHALL use proper HTML table structure (\`\u003ctable\u003e\`, \`\u003cthead\u003e\`, \`\u003ctbody\u003e\`).\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Range](https://gohugo.io/functions/go-template/range/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_WEEKLY_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Weekly Index Verification #BP_WEEKLY_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify Weekly Index displays all 52 weeks.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Navigate to \`/blog/weeks/\` → Expect page loads\n  - TS2: Count table rows → Expect 52 weeks\n  - TS3: Verify completed weeks → Expect linked with title\n  - TS4: Verify upcoming weeks → Expect not linked, muted styling\n  - TS5: Click completed week → Expect navigates to post\n  - TS6: Test in w3m → Expect table renders readably\n* **Dynamic Content:**\n  - Verify table updates when new weeks published\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_REPORTS_0001] - Blog Platform → Reports Section Implementation #BP021\n* Reports section SHALL be at \`content/blog/reports/_index.md\`.\n* Hugo template SHALL list all report posts (monthly, quarterly).\n* Reports SHALL be tagged or categorized for filtering.\n* Empty state SHALL display friendly message.\n* Report listing SHALL include: title, type (monthly/quarterly), date.\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Taxonomies](https://gohugo.io/content-management/taxonomies/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_REPORTS_TEST_0001] - TS2: Verify report listings → When reports exist\n  - TS3: Verify empty state → When no reports, friendly message\n  - TS4: Click report → Expect navigates to full report\n  - TS5: Verify type indicator → Monthly vs Quarterly distinguishable\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_COMMUNITY_0001] - Blog Platform → Community Page Implementation #BP022\n* Community page SHALL be at \`content/community/_index.md\`.\n* Page SHALL contain:\n  - Static introduction/description\n  - Dynamic repository list (JavaScript-populated)\n  - Fallback content when API unavailable\n* JavaScript SHALL fetch from GitHub Search API:\n  - Endpoint: \`https://api.github.com/search/repositories?q=topic:52vibes\`\n* API fetch SHALL be deferred (non-blocking page load).\n* References:\n  + [GitHub Search API](https://docs.github.com/en/rest/search/search?apiVersion=2022-11-28#search-repositories)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_COMMUNITY_TEST_0001] - TS2: Wait for API response → Expect repos displayed (if any)\n  - TS3: Verify loading indicator → During fetch\n  - TS4: Block API (DevTools) → Expect fallback displayed\n  - TS5: Disable JavaScript → Expect fallback link visible\n* **API Integration:**\n  - Verify correct endpoint called\n  - Verify topic filter applied\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_BLOGIDX_0001] - Blog Platform → Blog Index Implementation #BP023\n* Blog index SHALL be at \`content/blog/_index.md\`.\n* Hugo list template SHALL display all published posts.\n* Each listing SHALL show: title, date, summary/description.\n* Posts SHALL be ordered by date (newest first).\n* Hugo configuration: \`[params] mainSections = [\"blog\"]\`.\n* Pagination SHOULD be implemented if posts exceed 10.\n* References:\n  + [Hugo List Templates](https://gohugo.io/templates/lists/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_BLOGIDX_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Blog Index Verification #BP_BLOGIDX_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify blog index lists all posts.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Navigate to \`/blog/\` → Expect page loads\n  - TS2: Verify all published posts listed → Count matches\n  - TS3: Verify each listing → Title, date, summary present\n  - TS4: Verify ordering → Newest first\n  - TS5: Click post title → Expect navigates to full post\n  - TS6: Verify in CLI browser → List readable\n\n### URL Structure and Post Features (BP024, BP025, BP026, BP027, BP028, BP029, BP030)\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_URL_0001] - Blog Platform → Weekly Post URL Pattern #BP024\n* Weekly posts SHALL use URL pattern: \`/blog/week-XX-\u003cslug\u003e/\`\n* Week number SHALL be zero-padded (01-52).\n* Slug SHALL be derived from title (lowercase, hyphenated).\n* Hugo front matter SHALL define:\n  \`\`\`yaml\n  slug: \"week-01-infrastructure\"\n  \`\`\`\n* Alternatively, file naming: \`content/blog/week-01-infrastructure/index.md\`\n* References:\n  + [Hugo URL Management](https://gohugo.io/content-management/urls/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_URL_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Weekly Post URL Verification #BP_URL_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify weekly post URLs follow pattern.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Create week 1 post → Verify URL is \`/blog/week-01-\u003cslug\u003e/\`\n  - TS2: Verify zero-padding → Week 1 = 01, Week 10 = 10\n  - TS3: Verify slug format → Lowercase, hyphenated\n  - TS4: Test URL directly → Expect HTTP 200\n* **Boundary:**\n  - Week 01, Week 10, Week 52 formatting\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_URL_0002] - Blog Platform → Monthly Report URL Pattern #BP025\n* Monthly reports SHALL use URL pattern: \`/blog/reports/YYYY-MM/\`\n* Year: 4 digits, Month: 2 digits (zero-padded).\n* Content location: \`content/blog/reports/2026-01/index.md\`\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Content Organization](https://gohugo.io/content-management/organization/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_URL_TEST_0002] - Blog Platform → Monthly Report URL Verification #BP_URL_0002\n* **Objective:** Verify monthly report URLs follow pattern.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Create January 2026 report → Verify URL \`/blog/reports/2026-01/\`\n  - TS2: Verify date format → YYYY-MM\n  - TS3: Test URL directly → Expect HTTP 200\n* **Boundary:**\n  - January (01), December (12), year transitions\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_URL_0003] - Blog Platform → Quarterly Report URL Pattern #BP026\n* Quarterly reports SHALL use URL pattern: \`/blog/reports/YYYY-qN/\`\n* Year: 4 digits, Quarter: lowercase 'q' + 1-4.\n* Content location: \`content/blog/reports/2026-q1/index.md\`\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Content Organization](https://gohugo.io/content-management/organization/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_URL_TEST_0003] - Blog Platform → Quarterly Report URL Verification #BP_URL_0003\n* **Objective:** Verify quarterly report URLs follow pattern.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Create Q1 2026 report → Verify URL \`/blog/reports/2026-q1/\`\n  - TS2: Verify quarter format → Lowercase 'q' + 1-4\n  - TS3: Test all quarters → q1, q2, q3, q4\n* **Case Sensitivity:**\n  - Must be lowercase 'q', not 'Q'\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_META_0001] - Blog Platform → Post Metadata Display #BP027\n* Post template SHALL display metadata section at top.\n* Required metadata fields:\n  - Title (from front matter \`title\`)\n  - Publication date (from \`date\`, formatted human-readable)\n  - Reading time (calculated via Hugo, e.g., \`{{ .ReadingTime }} min read\`)\n  - Quarter/theme (from front matter \`quarter\` and \`theme\`)\n* Hugo template SHALL calculate reading time automatically.\n* Format example: \"Q1: Agentic Infrastructure • 5 min read • January 5, 2026\"\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Variables](https://gohugo.io/variables/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_META_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Post Metadata Verification #BP_META_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify post metadata is displayed correctly.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Navigate to blog post → Expect metadata section visible\n  - TS2: Verify title → Matches front matter\n  - TS3: Verify date → Human-readable format\n  - TS4: Verify reading time → Reasonable for content length\n  - TS5: Verify quarter/theme → Matches front matter\n* **Consistency:**\n  - Check multiple posts for consistent metadata display\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_POSTNAV_0001] - Blog Platform → Previous/Next Navigation #BP028\n* Post template SHALL include prev/next navigation links.\n* Hugo template SHALL use \`.PrevInSection\` and \`.NextInSection\`.\n* Links SHALL only appear when adjacent posts exist:\n  - No \"Previous\" on first post\n  - No \"Next\" on latest post\n* Link text SHALL include week number and/or title.\n* Navigation SHALL be positioned at end of post content.\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Page Methods](https://gohugo.io/methods/page/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_POSTNAV_TEST_0001] - Blog Platform → Post Navigation Verification #BP_POSTNAV_0001\n* **Objective:** Verify prev/next navigation works correctly.\n* **Test Steps:**\n  - TS1: Navigate to middle week → Expect both prev and next links\n  - TS2: Click Previous → Expect navigates to prior week\n  - TS3: Click Next → Expect navigates to following week\n  - TS4: Navigate to Week 1 → Expect NO previous link\n  - TS5: Navigate to latest week → Expect NO next link\n* **Edge Cases:**\n  - Single published week → No navigation links\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_SESSION_0001] - Blog Platform → Session Log Links #BP029\n* Post template SHALL include link to session log.\n* Link SHALL point to GitHub Wiki page for that week.\n* URL pattern: \`https://github.com/\u003cowner\u003e/\u003crepo\u003e/wiki/Week-XX-Session-Log\`\n* Link SHALL be labeled clearly (e.g., \"View Session Log\").\n* Link position: After post content, before comments section.\n* Hugo front matter MAY override default wiki URL.\n* References:\n  + [GitHub Wiki URLs](https://docs.github.com/en/communities/documenting-your-project-with-wikis)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_SESSION_TEST_0001] - TS2: Verify link label → Expect descriptive text\n  - TS3: Click link → Expect opens correct wiki page\n  - TS4: Verify wiki content → Expect relates to that week\n* **Link Validation:**\n  - Verify HTTP 200 response from wiki URL\n\nTECH_REQ: [BP_REPO_0001] - Blog Platform → Server-Side Rendering Architecture #BP002\n* All page content SHALL be rendered at build time by Hugo (Static Site Generation).\n* HTML output SHALL contain complete content without requiring JavaScript hydration.\n* No client-side templating frameworks (React, Vue, etc.) SHALL be used.\n* Hugo templates SHALL use Go template syntax for content rendering.\n* Template directory structure SHALL follow Hugo conventions:\n  - \`layouts/_default/baseof.html\` - base template\n  - \`layouts/_default/single.html\` - single content pages\n  - \`layouts/_default/list.html\` - list/index pages\n  - \`layouts/partials/\` - reusable template components\n* References:\n  + [Hugo Templates](https://gohugo.io/templates/)\n\nSYSTEST: [BP_SSR_TEST_0001] -
